</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Die Geschöpfe des Prometheus
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">The Creatures of Prometheus
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="pt">As Criaturas de Prometeu</span>; <span title="ja">プロメテウスの創造物</span>; <span title="pl">Twory Prometeusza</span>; <span title="ko">프로메테우스의 창조물</span>; <span title="ru">Творения Прометея</span>; <span class="expandline" title="7 more..."><span title="fr">Les Créatures de Prométhée</span>; <span title="es">Las criaturas de Prometeo</span>; <span title="fi">Prometheus</span>; <span title="uk">Творіння Прометея</span>; <span title="it">Le creature di Prometeo</span>; <span title="ca">Les criatures de Prometeu</span>; <span title="el">Τα πλάσματα του Προμηθέα</span></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="pl">Prometeusz</span>; <span title="nl">Die Geschopfe des Prometheus</span>; <span title="nl">Die Geschoepfe des Prometheus</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
